</span></span></span><![endif]><span style=3D'font-family:Consolas'>Paragra=
ph
Tags: Paragraphs are block-level elements<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=3DMsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle style=3D'text-indent:-.25in;mso-list:=

<p class=3DMsoListParagraphCxSpLast style=3D'text-indent:-.25in;mso-list:l1=

<p class=3DMsoNormal><span style=3D'font-family:Consolas'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p>=
</span></p>

<p class=3DMsoListParagraphCxSpFirst style=3D'margin-left:.25in;mso-add-spa=
ce:auto;
text-indent:-.25in;mso-list:l4 level1 lfo9'><![if !supportLists]><span

ont-family:
Wingdings'><span style=3D'mso-list:Ignore'>v<span style=3D'font:7.0pt "Time=
s New Roman"'>&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span style=3D'font-family:Consolas'>Block-l=
evel
elements<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=3DMsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle style=3D'text-indent:-.25in;mso-list:=
l4 level2 lfo9'><![if !supportLists]><span
style=3D'font-family:Wingdings;mso-fareast-font-family:Wingdings;mso-bidi-f=
ont-family:
Wingdings'><span style=3D'mso-list:Ignore'>&Oslash;<span style=3D'font:7.0p=
t "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span style=3D'font-family:Consolas'>HTML
(Hypertext Markup Language) elements are usually &quot;block-level&quot;
elements or &quot;inline&quot; elements. A block-level element occupies the
entire space of its parent element (container), thereby creating a
&quot;block.&quot;</span></p>

<p class=3DMsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle style=3D'text-indent:-.25in;mso-list:=
l4 level2 lfo9'><![if !supportLists]><span
style=3D'font-family:Wingdings;mso-fareast-font-family:Wingdings;mso-bidi-f=
ont-family:
Wingdings'><span style=3D'mso-list:Ignore'>&Oslash;<span style=3D'font:7.0p=
t "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span style=3D'font-family:Consolas'>Browsers
typically display the block-level element with a newline both before and af=
ter
the element.<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=3DMsoListParagraphCxSpLast style=3D'text-indent:-.25in;mso-list:l4=
 level2 lfo9'><![if !supportLists]><span
style=3D'font-family:Wingdings;mso-fareast-font-family:Wingdings;mso-bidi-f=
ont-family:
Wingdings'><span style=3D'mso-list:Ignore'>&Oslash;<span style=3D'font:7.0p=
t "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span style=3D'font-family:Consolas'>Block-l=
evel
elements may appear only within <span style=3D'mso-spacerun:yes'>&nbsp;</sp=
an>a
&lt;body&gt; element.<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=3DMsoNormal><span style=3D'font-family:Consolas'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p>=
</span></p>

<p class=3DMsoListParagraph style=3D'margin-left:.25in;mso-add-space:auto;
text-indent:-.25in;mso-list:l21 level1 lfo10'><![if !supportLists]><span

Wingdings'><span style=3D'mso-list:Ignore'>v<span style=3D'font:7.0pt "Time=
s New Roman"'>&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span style=3D'font-family:Consolas'>Section=
s: div
and span<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=3DMsoNormal><span style=3D'font-family:Consolas'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p>=
</span></p>

<p class=3DMsoListParagraphCxSpFirst style=3D'margin-left:.25in;mso-add-spa=
ce:auto;
text-indent:-.25in;mso-list:l21 level1 lfo10'><![if !supportLists]><span
style=3D'font-family:Wingdings;mso-fareast-font-family:Wingdings;mso-bidi-f=
ont-family:
Wingdings'><span style=3D'mso-list:Ignore'>v<span style=3D'font:7.0pt "Time=
s New Roman"'>&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span style=3D'font-family:Consolas'>The HTML
&lt;div&gt; element (or HTML Document Division Element) <o:p></o:p></span><=
/p>

<p class=3DMsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle style=3D'text-indent:-.25in;mso-list:=
l21 level2 lfo10'><![if !supportLists]><span
style=3D'font-family:Wingdings;mso-fareast-font-family:Wingdings;mso-bidi-f=
ont-family:
Wingdings'><span style=3D'mso-list:Ignore'>&Oslash;<span style=3D'font:7.0p=
t "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span style=3D'font-family:Consolas'>is the
generic container for flow content, which does not inherently represent
anything. <o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=3DMsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle style=3D'text-indent:-.25in;mso-list:=
l21 level2 lfo10'><![if !supportLists]><span
style=3D'font-family:Wingdings;mso-fareast-font-family:Wingdings;mso-bidi-f=
ont-family:
Wingdings'><span style=3D'mso-list:Ignore'>&Oslash;<span style=3D'font:7.0p=
t "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span style=3D'font-family:Consolas'>It can =
be
used to group elements for styling purposes (using the class or id attribut=
es),
or because they share attribute values, such as lang. <o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=3DMsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle style=3D'text-indent:-.25in;mso-list:=
l21 level2 lfo10'><![if !supportLists]><span
style=3D'font-family:Wingdings;mso-fareast-font-family:Wingdings;mso-bidi-f=
ont-family:
Wingdings'><span style=3D'mso-list:Ignore'>&Oslash;<span style=3D'font:7.0p=
t "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span style=3D'font-family:Consolas'>It shou=
ld be
used only when no other semantic element (such as &lt;article&gt; or
&lt;nav&gt;) is appropriate.<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=3DMsoListParagraphCxSpLast style=3D'text-indent:-.25in;mso-list:l2=
1 level2 lfo10'><![if !supportLists]><span
style=3D'font-family:Wingdings;mso-fareast-font-family:Wingdings;mso-bidi-f=
ont-family:
Wingdings'><span style=3D'mso-list:Ignore'>&Oslash;<span style=3D'font:7.0p=
t "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span style=3D'font-family:Consolas'>Example=
: &lt;div
style=3D&quot;background: skyblue;&quot;&gt;This is a div&lt;/div&gt;<o:p><=
/o:p></span></p>

<p class=3DMsoNormal><span style=3D'font-family:Consolas'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p>=
</span></p>

s New Roman"'>&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span style=3D'font-family:Consolas'>The HTML
&lt;span&gt; element <o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=3DMsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle style=3D'text-indent:-.25in;mso-list:=

t "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span style=3D'font-family:Consolas'>generic
inline container for phrasing content, which does not inherently represent
anything. <o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=3DMsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle style=3D'text-indent:-.25in;mso-list:=
l3 level2 lfo11'><![if !supportLists]><span

Wingdings'><span style=3D'mso-list:Ignore'>&Oslash;<span style=3D'font:7.0p=

</span></span></span><![endif]><span style=3D'font-family:Consolas'>It can =
be
used to group elements for styling purposes (using the class or id attribut=
es),
or because they share attribute values, such as lang. <o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=3DMsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle style=3D'text-indent:-.25in;mso-list:=
l3 level2 lfo11'><![if !supportLists]><span

Wingdings'><span style=3D'mso-list:Ignore'>&Oslash;<span style=3D'font:7.0p=
t "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span style=3D'font-family:Consolas'>It shou=
ld be
used only when no other semantic element is appropriate. <o:p></o:p></span>=
</p>

<p class=3DMsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle style=3D'text-indent:-.25in;mso-list:=
l3 level2 lfo11'><![if !supportLists]><span
style=3D'font-family:Wingdings;mso-fareast-font-family:Wingdings;mso-bidi-f=
ont-family:
Wingdings'><span style=3D'mso-list:Ignore'>&Oslash;<span style=3D'font:7.0p=
t "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span style=3D'font-family:Consolas'>&lt;spa=
n&gt;
is very much like a &lt;div&gt; element, but &lt;div&gt; is a block-level
element whereas a &lt;span&gt; is an inline element.<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=3DMsoListParagraphCxSpLast style=3D'text-indent:-.25in;mso-list:l3=

t "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span style=3D'font-family:Consolas'>cellpad=
ding -
Defines the empty space around the cell content<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=3DMsoNormal><span style=3D'font-family:Consolas'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p>=

</span></span></span><![endif]><span style=3D'font-family:Consolas'>Cells h=
ave
two attributes related to merging<o:p></o:p></span></p>

</span></span></span><![endif]><span style=3D'font-family:Consolas'>colspan=
 -
Defines how many columns the cell occupies<o:p></o:p></span></p>

s New Roman"'>&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span style=3D'font-family:Consolas'>&lt;nof=
rames&gt;<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=3DMsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle style=3D'text-indent:-.25in;mso-list:=
l14 level2 lfo19'><![if !supportLists]><span
style=3D'font-family:Wingdings;mso-fareast-font-family:Wingdings;mso-bidi-f=
ont-family:
Wingdings'><span style=3D'mso-list:Ignore'>&Oslash;<span style=3D'font:7.0p=
t "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span style=3D'font-family:Consolas'>HTML el=
ement
which is used to supporting browsers which are not able to support
&lt;frame&gt; elements or configured to do so.<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=3DMsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle style=3D'text-indent:-.25in;mso-list:=
l14 level2 lfo19'><![if !supportLists]><span
style=3D'font-family:Wingdings;mso-fareast-font-family:Wingdings;mso-bidi-f=
ont-family:
Wingdings'><span style=3D'mso-list:Ignore'>&Oslash;<span style=3D'font:7.0p=
t "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><b><span style=3D'font-family:Consolas'>Note=
:</span></b><span
style=3D'font-family:Consolas'> Because of the fact that all mainstream bro=
wsers
support frames, usage of this element is not necessary in general cases. It=
 is
also entirely obsolete in HTML5 and should be avoided to conform to the
standard.<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=3DMsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle style=3D'text-indent:-.25in;mso-list:=
l14 level2 lfo19'><![if !supportLists]><span

</span></span></span><![endif]><b style=3D'mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><sp=
an
style=3D'font-family:Consolas'>Example:<o:p></o:p></span></b></p>

<p class=3DMsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle style=3D'margin-left:35.4pt;mso-add-s=
pace:
auto'><span style=3D'font-size:9.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:=
Consolas'>&lt;frameset
cols=3D&quot;50%,50%&quot;&gt;<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=3DMsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle style=3D'margin-left:53.4pt;mso-add-s=
pace:
auto'><span style=3D'font-size:9.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:=

src=3D&quot;https://developer.mozilla.org/en/HTML/Element/frameset&quot; /&=
gt;<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=3DMsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle style=3D'margin-left:53.4pt;mso-add-s=

auto'><span style=3D'font-size:9.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:=

src=3D&quot;https://developer.mozilla.org/en/HTML/Element/frame&quot; /&gt;=
<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=3DMsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle style=3D'margin-left:53.4pt;mso-add-s=
pace:
auto'><span style=3D'font-size:9.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:=
Consolas'>&lt;noframes&gt;&lt;p&gt;It
seems your browser does not support frames or configured to does not
so.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/noframes&gt;<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=3DMsoListParagraphCxSpLast style=3D'margin-left:35.4pt;mso-add-spa=
ce:auto'><span

t;/frameset&gt;<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=3DMsoNormal><span style=3D'font-family:Consolas'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p>=
</span></p>

<p class=3DMsoListParagraphCxSpFirst style=3D'margin-left:.25in;mso-add-spa=
ce:auto;

ont-family:
Wingdings'><span style=3D'mso-list:Ignore'>v<span style=3D'font:7.0pt "Time=
s New Roman"'>&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span style=3D'font-family:Consolas'>The HTML
Inline Frame Element (&lt;iframe&gt;) <o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=3DMsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle style=3D'text-indent:-.25in;mso-list:=
l26 level2 lfo20'><![if !supportLists]><span
style=3D'font-family:Wingdings;mso-fareast-font-family:Wingdings;mso-bidi-f=
ont-family:
Wingdings'><span style=3D'mso-list:Ignore'>&Oslash;<span style=3D'font:7.0p=
t "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span style=3D'font-family:Consolas'>represe=
nts a
nested browsing context, effectively embedding another HTML page into the
current page. <o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=3DMsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle style=3D'text-indent:-.25in;mso-list:=
l26 level2 lfo20'><![if !supportLists]><span
style=3D'font-family:Wingdings;mso-fareast-font-family:Wingdings;mso-bidi-f=
ont-family:
Wingdings'><span style=3D'mso-list:Ignore'>&Oslash;<span style=3D'font:7.0p=
t "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span style=3D'font-family:Consolas'>In HTML=
 4.01,
a document may contain a head and a body or a head and a frame-set, but not
both a body and a frame-set. However, an &lt;iframe&gt; can be used within a
normal document body. <o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=3DMsoListParagraphCxSpLast style=3D'text-indent:-.25in;mso-list:l2=
6 level2 lfo20'><![if !supportLists]><span
style=3D'font-family:Wingdings;mso-fareast-font-family:Wingdings;mso-bidi-f=
ont-family:
Wingdings'><span style=3D'mso-list:Ignore'>&Oslash;<span style=3D'font:7.0p=
t "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span style=3D'font-family:Consolas'>Each br=
owsing
context has its own session history and active document.<o:p></o:p></span><=
/p>

<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=3DMsoNormal style=3D'margin-left:.25in'><span style=3D'font-family=
:Consolas'>Web
1.0 refers to the first stage in the World Wide Web, which was entirely mad=
e up
of Web pages connected by hyperlinks. Although the exact definition of Web =
1.0
is a source of debate, it is generally believed to refer to the Web when it=
 was
a set of static websites that were not yet providing interactive content. In
Web 1.0, applications were also generally proprietary.<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=3DMsoNormal><span style=3D'font-family:Consolas'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p>=
</span></p>

<p class=3DMsoListParagraph style=3D'margin-left:.25in;mso-add-space:auto;

s New Roman"'>&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span style=3D'font-family:Consolas'>Web 2.0=
<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=3DMsoNormal style=3D'margin-left:.25in'><span style=3D'font-family=
:Consolas'>Web
2.0 is the name used to the describe the second generation of the World Wide
Web, where it moved static HTML pages to a more interactive and dynamic Web
experience. Web 2.0 is focused on the ability for people to collaborate and
share information online via social media, blogging and Web-based communiti=
es.<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<o:p></o:p></span></p>

t "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span style=3D'font-family:Consolas'>Internet
Information Services (IIS, formerly Internet Information Server) is an
extensible web server created by Microsoft for use with Windows NT family.[=
2]
IIS supports HTTP, HTTPS, FTP, FTPS, SMTP and NNTP. It has been an integral
part of the Windows NT family since Windows NT 4.0, though it may be absent
from some editions (e.g. Windows XP Home edition). IIS is not turned on by
default when Windows is installed. The IIS Manager is accessed through the
Microsoft Management Console or Administrative Tools in the Control Panel.<=
o:p></o:p></span></p>

</span></span></span><![endif]><span style=3D'font-family:Consolas'>A secure
service to process business transactions.<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=3DMsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle style=3D'margin-left:.75in;mso-add-sp=
ace:
auto;text-indent:-.25in;mso-list:l23 level3 lfo30'><![if !supportLists]><sp=

"Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span style=3D'font-family:Consolas'>A servi=
ce
that supplies current data to others, such as a traffic report or other
monitoring service.<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=3DMsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle style=3D'margin-left:.75in;mso-add-sp=
ace:

</span></span></span><![endif]><span style=3D'font-family:Consolas'>A chat
service that allows two people to communicate or exchange data in real time=

<p class=3DMsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle style=3D'margin-left:.75in;mso-add-sp=

</span></span></span><![endif]><span style=3D'font-family:Consolas'>A dashb=

<p class=3DMsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle style=3D'margin-left:.75in;mso-add-sp=
